11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截止<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3509</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">九年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">九年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">109</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整九年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">4</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">9</span>千字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">41</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留和被精神病的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">28</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1656</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，退休职工。她的丈夫孟凡胜，六十岁，退伍军人，家住河北省衡水市景县。夫妇俩在北京帮助儿子看孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，孟凡胜和崔永芬夫妇在北京海淀区一小区内照看四岁的孙子，发放法轮功真相卡片，被人恶意举报，遭跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，崔永芬和孟凡胜在他们的儿子家被北京市海淀区公安分局和田村路派出所警察抓捕，被抄家，被关押到北京海淀看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，孟凡胜被释放，回到在北京的儿子家。崔永芬继续被关押在北京海淀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌多项罪名正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被以拉萨市中级法院以“阻止政府在‘纳拉赞巴’圣上开矿”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，以“私下向他人贷款罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，以“妨碍公务罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。目前被关押在拉萨扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，是退休工人，家住天津市河东区泰安大街<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日上午八点左右，她在家中被天津市河东区国保与中山门派出所警察抓捕，关押在河东区看守所。据警察称，李兰敏发放真相资料被人告了，经查看监控摄像头、追踪找到她的住处。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被中级法院驳回上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转监到天津市女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span lang="EN-US">80</span>年代从事业余新闻报道工作，到<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代末从事专业新闻报道工作。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日创办中国舆论监督网，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发布《下跪的副市长——山东济宁市副市长李信丑行录》，<span lang="EN-US">46</span>天后，李信被逮捕，最终被判无期徒刑。李新德成为新闻界的新闻人物，被誉为中国民间舆论监督第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人。李新德利用网络反腐维权的事迹，许多媒体均与报道。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，江苏省邳州市公安局以李新德涉嫌“经营罪”指定居所监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月后的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日转为刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日经邳州市检察院批准逮捕。现羁押在邳州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，江苏省邳州市法院以“经营罪”判处“中国舆论监督网”创办人李新德有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李新德刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西安法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年生。李雪松老太太<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在<span lang="EN-US">236</span>、<span lang="EN-US">207</span>路公交车上宣讲法轮功时被人举报。未央区公安分局国保大队指定徐家湾派出所对她实施抓捕。之后李雪松被逮捕，案件移送至检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其被西安市莲湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金一万。其本人不服枉判，已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">13/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk181061851"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明洁</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孟素英：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员。孙广利、孟素英夫妇，黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市碾子山区人，暂住辽宁省沈阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多孙广利、孟素英夫妇，在沈阳市辽中区<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房镇的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个村子里发了几张告诉世人如何躲避瘟疫的方法，被人诬告，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房派出所的警察将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕到当地派出所进行关押。 由于那时中国疫情严重，看守所不接收，次日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人放回家中。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，东街派出所的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个警察又到家中将夫妻<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人强行抓捕到东街派出所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，丈夫孙广利被关押到沈阳第二看守所，妻子孟素英被关押到沈阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日傍晚，他们的家人接到法院通知：孙广利、孟素英夫妇判决已下来，最终两人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: 0pt;">山东东营市法轮功学员，女，山东东营市胜利一中（原七中）历史老师，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被滨海公安局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东东营区法院对孟昱进行了庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，孟昱被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃永沛：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广西人权律师。覃永沛是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被注销律师牌照。由他主持，曾代理过不少维权案件的”百举鸣律师事务所”，被勒令解散后，转为法律咨询公司的形式，继续提供法律服务。覃永沛也连同多名维权律师，成立“中国律师后俱乐部”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月末，覃永沛所属原律师事务所律师陈家鸿被玉林警方拘留，罪名为“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。当时覃永沛曾积极作出声援及呼吁放人，目前陈家鸿律师尚在羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日傍晚五点左右，南宁警方十数人闯入原百举鸣律师事务所（现百永鸣法律咨询服务有限公司）办公室，将该所原主任、人权律师后覃永沛控制并带走，同时覃的办公室被警方查封。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛被指涉煽动颠覆国家政权罪遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月案件移送检察院审查起诉。已经进入审判阶段，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日开庭。现关押在南宁第二看守所。覃永沛案被最高法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日决定再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，广西南宁中院<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日才通知律师。此前，覃永沛律师妻子也是其代理辩护人于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号寄了取保候审申请书后到现在，准或不准，没有任何通知，法律明文规定三日之内作出书面答复的。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛煽动颠覆国家政权案一审宣判，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，山东聊城水城集团退休，修炼法轮功后，身心受益。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，孙玉斌在聊城财干路贴法轮功不干胶时，遭东昌府区香江派出所抓捕。警察晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点抄他家，抢走了大法书、电脑等。孙玉斌被关押在茌平区看守所构陷。关押半年，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被聊城市东阿县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。因中共肺炎的原因，他还被关押在聊城看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E8%81%8A%E5%9F%8E%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E5%AD%99%E7%8E%89%E6%96%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441291.html"><span _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在家中被抓捕，第二天回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次在家中被警察抓捕，之后遭当地中共公检法人员的司法构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份被大连普兰店法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，现在被关在普兰店看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被环县环城派出所警察从家中抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，王明全被环县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经八十二岁<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，王玉和因修炼法轮功，被判三年。当时在极大的压力下，王玉和出现了高血压和脑血栓两种高危病症，导致半身不遂，生活不能自理，被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，王玉和回到家中。此后，法院刑事庭庭长孙锡河接管王玉和案，再次下达收监令。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，大连市办案队警察闯到她女儿家，在王玉和独自在家之时，抓捕了她。被关押折磨一年半后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，家人探视发现王玉和身体虚弱，举步维艰，需要人搀扶。见此，女儿为已<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的母亲申请保外就医，监狱拒收她的申请。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/26/%E4%B8%AD%E5%85%B1%E5%86%A4%E7%8D%84%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8%E5%85%AB%E6%97%AC%E7%8E%8B%E7%8E%89%E5%92%8C-%E5%AE%B6%E5%B1%AC%E7%94%B3%E8%AB%8B%E4%BF%9D%E5%A4%96%E5%B0%B1%E9%86%AB%E8%A2%AB%E6%8B%92%E6%94%B6-464587.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk181062340"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王忠胜</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺市新宾县法轮功学员。曾在新宾县中共党校任教，高级讲师，三十多年的工龄，只因为修炼法轮功，坚持自己的信仰，被开除公职，多次被抓捕，关进劳教所和洗脑班迫害。为了维持生活，他曾经不得不靠走街串巷磨剪子菜刀艰难度日，后靠辅导学生谋生。二十多年来，他和妻子王桂兰饱尝了迫害给他们造成的所有经济损失、精神损失之苦，妻子王桂兰于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份离开人世。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被新宾县国保抓捕、抄家，后于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金四千元，曾被关押在抚顺南沟看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。王忠胜，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已七十五岁，现被关押在沈阳市东陵监狱三监区，他因被迫害严重，生命垂危，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月在监狱医院住院。据知情人透露：王忠胜被狱警逼坐小凳，不让活动，臀部溃烂，越来越严重。该知情者说，已无法治愈<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">80</span>后，四川达州公民，长期在福建南安工作生活。热心公义，多年来坚持传播常识，致力推动社会进步，构建公民社会。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在厦门大学门口拉横幅呼吁释放许志永、黄琦、李怀庆、王臧、余文生、程渊、丁家喜、张展等良心犯。并宣传人权、民主、法治等理念，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被福建省南安是警方抓捕。在没有通知家属的情况，被当局以“寻衅滋事”的名义秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，截止目前家属都未曾收到判决书。肖春已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日移送至福建省漳州监狱服刑。目前其夫人需要照顾家里的<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个孩子和一个老人，成了家里唯一的顶梁柱，一家人生活十分拮据。漳州监狱已疫情为由，停止会见，无奈家属只能写信。但信寄出逾三个月了，没有任何回音，家属非常挂念并担心肖的身体，呼吁当局保障肖春通信等基本权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p lang="EN-US">3</span>月因讲法轮功被人举报，曾多次被北辰区瑞景派出所抓捕：有时被劫持去法院；有时去检察院；有时去多个地方检查身体。每次都是经肖树清讲真相当天放回或几天后放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，肖树清又被北辰瑞景派出所抓捕抽血、检查身体；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，现被关押在北辰看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功，姚桂珍在上海黄浦公园炼功，被拘留一个月；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年腊月，姚桂珍和十几岁的儿子（儿子还在读中学）遭绑架、抄家，未成年的儿子被关押一个月后，被劫持到上海青浦“洗脑班”迫害。姚桂珍被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，关押在上海女子劳教所，长时间被“关小号”，精神和肉体遭受严重的摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，姚桂珍遭抓捕，被关押到上海市宝山区看守所。后遭批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，姚桂珍被静安区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日抓捕了包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，包万明、滕淑丽、周克铭被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被非法关押在鸡西市看守所<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。包万明、周克铭、滕淑丽，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭鸡东法院以视频的方式开庭，近日得知，包万明被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、罚金十万元；滕淑丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元；周克铭被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。周克铭刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，何世国被邯郸市公安局国保大队、永年分局国保大队联合抓捕，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉，其被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/04/16_16.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">37/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王伟才：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东省人，佛山市顺德区公民，基督徒，曾为个体经商者，后为广东顺德盛佳家庭教会全职服事同工，“盛佳共学互助中心”培训员，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年皈依基督教以来，因秉承信仰，诚心参与教会聚会、敬拜活动并经常帮助教友排忧解难，而深得教牧同工及教友们的喜爱；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因其立定全身心投入福音的传播活动，故而毅然放下自己的生意而在顺德盛佳家庭教会做全职服事同工；因其在教会从事同工活动过程中，认识到盛佳教会虽属家庭教会，但在法律上却是受国家宗教自由白皮书明文保护的合法教会，并且其教会内部印刷的一些与圣经相关培训学习数据也不未违法，遂经常向教会信徒及其亲友、慕道友（即常到教会听道，但未受洗的信仰追求者）等人推介和共同学习这些与圣经根本不违背的内部数据；然而近年来，因中共当局修订并强化了对《宗教事务条例》的管理，佛山市民宗局遂频繁前往盛佳家庭教会，要求教会加入和接受中共所属的“三自教会”管辖，但因被其等教牧同工多次拒绝，遂屡遭地方当局上门骚扰、警告；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，盛佳教会开设的“盛佳共学互助中心”（即圣经学习培训班）突遭顺德区警方、民宗局和小区人员等数十人的联合查处，教会所用教学设备及学习数据全被没收，教会大门被查封，其与传道人邓燕祥和教会同工朱江龙、朱巧玲等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被警方带走；次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日），其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被顺德区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其等又被顺德区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控他们因让教会信徒和培训学生使用教会内部印刷的圣经学习数据，故此行为与国家新修订《宗教管理条例》相抵触，应被逮捕和法办；据悉，其被抓至今一直无更多解体信息，只知其家人生活、工作等面临极大压力，教会其余未被抓捕同工和信徒仍持续被警方约谈；又悉，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其教会朱龙飞长老也被顺德区警察以同罪名刑拘，并送同一看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，广东省佛山市顺德区人民法院作出了对广东顺德盛佳教会王伟才执事取保候审的决定，王伟才目前已经离开看守所与家人团聚。此前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_55.html</span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_51.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">38/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖南省长沙市岳麓区人，网名：<span lang="EN-US">@</span>铁子，推号：<span lang="EN-US">@fanjunyidu</span>，职业不详，多项公益活动组织者及参与者，“中国国民党”忠实粉丝，网络活跃人士，“墙外信息搬运工”，长沙“同城饭醉”活动参与者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾组织参与多项公益活动，包括关爱山区学童、定时组织探望敬老院老人及参与公益百公里志愿者活动等，故而深得资助者和维权公民称许和认可；又因其是国军后代，长期坚定支持和拥护三民主义及国民党发到墙内，再由其创建的微信群和<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传发，而屡遭长沙当局打压；曾因按月例行组织并参与“同城饭醉”活动，以及组织经常性的举牌抗议活动等，而被长沙市警方多次“喝茶”、传唤和拘留处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因参与长沙同城公民七月聚餐后举牌声援<span lang="EN-US">709</span>律师和公民，并将举牌照片发到网上，而立遭长沙市岳麓区警方约谈“喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因将“美国之音”网站的文图信息转发到微信群组，再次遭岳麓区警方传唤做笔录，其家被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因举牌要求中共结束一党专政，允许人民在推特发表言论，而被岳麓区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-29</span>日，又因公民聚餐后举牌抗议中共花纳税人的钱举行大阅兵，而被岳麓区警方以“扰乱公共秩序”罪由再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其突然被云南省警方跨省抓捕，次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日）被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，自此失联；对其被抓，外界曾一度怀疑与“六四”将至，当局恐其会有所动作，以及其近期网络言论和在微信群立转发内容有关，其被持续拘押不放，据悉，其被拘捕更多可能与涉及“武装”、“武装组织”或与此类似的案件有关；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月遭云南省警方跨省抓捕的湖南民主人士樊钧益已经获释出狱。一直以来，因云南警方拒不答复外界友人对其案情的问询，而其家人又因恐遭警方威胁而选择对外缄默不语，故其更多信息缺详。此前被羁押于云南省昆明市某看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_14.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_14.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/20205.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">39/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk181063885"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">葛志慧</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，北京市丰台区人，丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院公民，维权残疾人士，实名举报人，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，其商业用房曾遭政府暴力强拆，财产被洗劫一空，并长期未作任何补偿与安置；因其做合理抗争，反被对方殴打致残，遂被迫拄着双拐、拖着残疾的身体走上维权诉讼之路，却又因此多次被非法拘禁，遭数次行政拘留和刑事拘留等疯狂打击和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因维权控诉而遭地方当局及其所雇社会闲杂人员非法闯入家中，将其打昏拖走；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年初，曾因抗暴维权惨遭毒打致残，多次上访毫无果效反遭打击报复，致其生活陷入极度困境之中；曾因多次到区政府寻求救助，竟被百般推诿，故在绝望之下，选择跳楼自杀，幸被及时救治，幸免遇难；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因声援人权律师浦志强案而被丰台区警方殴打，致其右腿韧带损伤，且长时得不到医治；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因向中国人民代表大会谏言，要求对香港《<span lang="EN-US">831</span>决定》进行违宪审查，随遭传唤拘押<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多个小时，并被要求不准再说香港之事；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾为免受地方当局暗中迫害，被迫露宿街头，艰难度日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其和同区维权者李美青到中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府黑社会化强拆问题，而遭到丰台区维稳人员的阻截；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市丰台区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家被查抄；后又被丰台区检察院以同罪名转正式批捕和起诉，指控其曾因去北京市丰台区政府门口上访、去北京市<span lang="EN-US">999</span>急救中心探望 维权人士曹顺利、在丰台区郑常庄村委会换界选举现场发表相关意见、上网发布有关维权活动信息等等，故而触犯了政府相关法律；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在北京市丰台区法院开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，终被该法院通过视频方式一审以“寻衅滋事罪”被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；刑满释放；据悉，看守所关押期间其曾多次被狱中欺凌。此前在北京市天河监狱（北京市大兴区天堂河庆丰路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号<span lang="EN-US">1290-10</span>信箱，邮编<span lang="EN-US">102609</span>，电话<span lang="EN-US"> 1600628</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，葛志慧又被北京市公安局丰台分局以寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，被关押在北京丰台区看守所。据悉其“寻衅滋事”罪状是将自己历年来被传唤、行拘、刑拘、判刑的判决书等法律文书放到了快手网络上。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，获悉：葛志慧女士日前已取保获释回家。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱龙飞：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东顺德盛佳教会长老。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，广东顺德盛佳教会朱龙飞长老被佛山市顺德区公安局以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑事拘留。羁押在佛山市南海区看守所。广东顺德盛佳教会朱龙飞长老等五位基督徒被控涉非法经营案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日结束庭审。朱龙江朱巧玲兄妹在<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日就取保回家。但此案的审判结果至今未出。<a name="_Hlk179332403"><span lang="EN-US">2024</span></a>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，广东省佛山市顺德区人民法院作出了对顺德盛佳教会朱龙飞长老取保候审的决定。他已平安回家，见到了妻子梁丹丹、此前被取保的哥哥朱龙江、姐姐朱巧玲以及其他弟兄姊妹。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">41/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk181065567"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">谢文飞</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本名谢丰夏。 <span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖南省郴州市桂阳县人，网名“谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞”、“南街谢文飞<span lang="EN-US">@njxwf </span>”，人权捍卫者，南方街头运动践行者，政治犯。近年来，因经常活跃于广州街头，勇于为推动中国的民主宪政事业积极发声和献身，故而遭到广东当局的多次打压和拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因前往围观广州公民李伊国申请“六四游行”被拘提起诉讼案开庭，而被广东省佛山市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，关押于佛山市禅诚区看守所，事由是“纪念林昭和曹顺利”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，曾因与民主维权公民王福磊、王默等在广州举牌，发起寻找民主异见人士张圣雨的活动，被石围派出所警方带走，且被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，曾因穿着黑衫在广州市街头拉横幅声援香港民主抗争、“真普选”，被广州警方从增城区新塘镇住所再次带走，并以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；审讯期间，遭酷刑折磨，被广州市越秀看守所警方实施“定镣”处罚，时间长达<span lang="EN-US">104</span>个小时；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，被广州市检察院更换罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式批捕，并被转关至广州市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其案正式开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被广州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放。此前在广东省河源监狱服刑。谢文飞于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日晚上在苏仙区租房处被郴州警方强制带走，次日苏仙区公安分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事为由将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日其被办案单位苏仙区公安分局移送苏仙区检察院审查起诉，后检察院以谢文飞“涉嫌寻衅滋事”罪向苏仙区法院起诉。谢文飞羁押在郴州市下辖的资兴市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日开庭。一直未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月宣判，谢文飞获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后被转监到湖南长沙赤山监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
