style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">何方美、</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">杨泽伟（网名乔鑫鑫）</span></span><a name="_Hlk170538828"></a><a name="_Hlk162565472"></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">余文生<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">许艳<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">何方美简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，河南省新乡市辉县人，网名“十三妹”，“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人，人权捍卫者，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年度“曹顺利人权捍卫者奖共同获得者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其年仅<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月龄的小女打了百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助投诉均被拒，遂逐级维权讨说法，后因多地亦发生类似疫苗伤害宝宝事件，随组建“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体共同呼吁，以求当局关注并给予合理赔偿救治；然当局却对此一拖再拖，其被迫到北京上访，故屡遭抓捕打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，因中共两会期间与各地问题疫苗家长到北京王府井为残儿募捐，随被新乡市辉县警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被以辉县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转刑拘，关押在河南省新乡市看守所；因期间一直拒绝认罪，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新乡市辉县检察院以同罪名批捕，后被起诉并罗列<span lang="EN-US">6</span>项罪，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其案在河南省辉县法院正式开庭；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被辉县检察院以“事实不清、证据不足”为由撤诉，后被无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因其不断发声请求国家立法解决疫苗问题、呼吁联合国关注中国疫苗问题等，而在北京再度遭遇强迫失踪；释放后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因当地政府阻挠其带疫苗致残的女儿看病，随对辉县政府招牌泼墨抗议，而被行政拘留；后于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日第二次对辉县市政府泼漆抗议；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，知其及其丈夫、六岁的儿子、三岁的残疾女儿一起被警方软禁，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其被河南省辉县市警方以涉嫌“重婚罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；据悉，羁押期间，其产下一女，有关部门已致电其家属，称若不去领回孩子，其所有孩子将被送到福利院。目前被羁押于河南省新乡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河南辉县警察骗遭软禁的何方美说快要放她了，带她出去拍照体检，结果第二天直接把何方美带去参加庭审。她被当庭逮捕。其亲属接到逮捕通知后立刻聘请了律师。可律师来辉县法院时，法院以案件已经开过庭，审判委员会已经讨论过了为由，拒绝律师阅卷。辉县法院连律师阅卷都不准许，本案谈何公正处理？何方美多年来致力于疫苗群体维权。其实她自己也有听力残障，即天生没有耳廓、耳洞，需要大声或者看唇语来跟别人交流。本案在辉县法院开庭时，法院只让她听审，拒绝她看任何书面材料。她当庭才知丈夫李新被以寻衅滋事罪、重婚罪判了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年多，已在服刑中。何在开庭时解除了法援律师，提交了<span lang="EN-US">50</span>页的自辩词。自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日“疫苗宝宝之家”发起人、人权捍卫者何方美被抓捕羁押，至今已超过<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，辉县法院在新乡看守所一审宣判何方美案，何方美被以重婚罪、寻衅滋事罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。何方美自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月起被监视居住长达<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，本案<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月一审开庭后，迟迟不下判长达<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月。而其两个年幼女儿目前仍然下落不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_25.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/blog-post_25.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/456.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/456.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨泽伟：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">网名乔鑫鑫，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖南省衡阳祁东县人，客居老挝中国公民，新闻媒体人，前广州市某新闻媒体职员，前自由亚洲电台驻东南亚特约记者，中国拆墙运动（<span lang="EN-US">BanGFW</span>）发起人，“拆墙宝典”写作和推动者，海外民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。大学时期，曾因看到长达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个小时的六四大屠杀影片而深感震撼，故自此频繁接触美国人，并在一家驻华美国文化中心作兼职人员，以了解和体悟到中国宣传的虚假与邪恶；大学毕业后，曾因到广东省广州市做新闻工作者，故而积极利用职业之便经常在美国总领事馆参加文化讲座活动；曾参加<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年美国总统大选观摩会和，并阅览一年香港英文日报，使自己知晓更多与中国官方新闻报导相左的信息，并深切体会、感悟到新闻真实性报导的重要性；曾因中共自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末起开始建起网络长城防火墙（<span lang="EN-US">Great Firewall</span>，简称：<span lang="EN-US">GFW</span>），实行互联网边界网络审查系统，而使其在中国境内使用手机和计算机时深感防火墙给其及国人阅览设限带来的困扰；后其移居老挝生活，并学习了十种语言；曾因中国逐渐成为世界最大的电子监狱，为了维稳不惜每年花费巨<span lang="EN-US">60</span>亿美元打造网络防火墙，封锁了<span lang="EN-US">Google</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Youtube</span>、<span lang="EN-US">BBC</span>、<span lang="EN-US">CNN</span>等全球<span lang="EN-US">31</span>万个网站，造成国人只能接触中共的洗脑讯息，而且，近年来因中国将防火墙技术输出到俄罗斯、伊朗、缅甸、柬埔寨等国，迫使十几亿人每天无端地去仇美、反日、攻台，造成了全球冲突连绵不断，遂其据此开始致力于把新兴的拆墙运动（<span lang="EN-US">BanGFW</span>）理念向多国推广，呼吁大家都来举牌、发帖；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其等海外民主派人士发起拆墙运动，并推出《拆墙宝典》，争取国际社会各方支持，以期达到将中共主管建立和运作防火墙的首要份子提交海牙国际刑事法院的要求；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，其六四<span lang="EN-US">34</span>周年纪念日前夕的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，突遭中国警方跨境抓捕；后知其在当地侨领、老挝警方的连手配合下被中国警方野蛮绑架，自此失联，后证实其已被押回湖南衡阳，目前羁押在湖南衡阳市未成年人看守所。杨泽伟于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年是<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被衡阳市检察院批捕，其罪名是“煽颠颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日获悉，其一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月移送湖南赤山监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/5.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3 /</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">余文生</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，北京市人，前北京市隆聚律师事务所主任、前北京市律师协会青年委员会委员，原北京市道衡律师事务所律师，北京知名人权律师。曾获<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年法德人权法治奖、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年马丁<span lang="EN-US">.</span>恩纳尔斯奖、<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年安娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>达尔贝克奖。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因为中国奥运的知识产权事宜付出了巨大努力，而荣获北京市律师协会颁发的“律师行业奥运工作突出贡献奖”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾被评为北京市石景山律协律师代表；近年来，曾因高度关注弱势群体，为多起维权案件当事人作过代理律师（如基督徒徐彩虹、何斌案、王春艳姊妹敲诈政府案，浙江维权代表朱瑛娣案，李英之案，拆迁上访者赵勇案，著名律师王成诉律协和法制日报案等），而受到业界及维权群体的普遍好评和欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因前往黑龙江省牡丹江市看守所要求会见当事人（即被关押的法轮功信仰者），而被警方非法抓进看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，因前往监狱迎接因要求官员财产公示而获刑的维权公民袁冬出狱，而遭到当局的再次不满；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因前往预约会见因声援香港占中事件被羁押于北京市丰台看守所的维权公民张宗钢，遭到拒绝后将实情发到网上，遂于又一次遭到当局的强烈不满和恶意打击，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日即被北京市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被北京市大兴区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；其妻曾先后委托<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名律师近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>次要求会见余文生，均被当局以“需要向市局汇报、案件涉及国家秘密”为由拒绝，直至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，终获取保释放；获释后，曾遭多次当局骚扰和暗示，令其不能正常找到工作；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因此前在看守所时患上小肠疝气，又受到狱警酷刑虐待及饥饿折磨，其随向北京市大兴区检察院正式提出要求国家赔偿申请，孰料<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日却等来一份来自北京市司法局注销其律师资格证的决定书；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被北京市石景山警方以涉嫌“妨碍公务罪”再次刑拘，关押于石景山看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被江苏省徐州市铜山区警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被徐州市警方以同罪名正式逮捕，并被羁押于徐州市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其案在徐州市中级法院秘密开庭，但久拖不判；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，终被该法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服上诉；二审依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，狱中其身患严重慢性疾病，长期医治无效，又因双手颤抖残疾愈加严重，故其生活难以自理。此前在江苏省南京监狱老残监区服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，欧盟外交与安全政策高级代表博雷利及德国外长贝尔伯克访问中国。余文生和妻子许艳在当天下午应邀前往德国大使馆。然而，他们在北京搭乘地铁时遭到多名便衣警察的拦截，并被口头传唤。随后，余文生和许艳被带到北京石景山八角派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，余文生夫妇均被刑事拘留，罪名是“寻衅滋事”。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚，超过<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名警察到余文生的住处，向其刚满<span lang="EN-US">18</span>岁的儿子宣读余文生律师及其妻子许艳被刑事拘留的通知，不给书面文件也不允许拍照。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，余文生律师夫妇以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪正式批捕。此前余文生、许艳一直关押在北京市石景山区看守所，后被追加“煽动颠覆国家政权”罪。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初获悉，余文生及其妻子许艳被从北京转至苏州关押，目前余文生关押于苏州市第一看守所，许艳关押于同地点的苏州市第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余文生、许艳案开庭，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日宣判，余文生获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，许艳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。余文生刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><a name="_Hlk181146269"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New _Hlk181146269;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181146269;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许艳：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，天津市人，北京市石景山区八角北路<span lang="EN-US">24</span>楼租住居民，人权律师余文生之妻，基督徒，推特账号<span lang="EN-US">l@xuyan709</span>，<span lang="EN-US"> 709</span>维权系列案家属之一，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自从与人权律师余文生结婚以后，夫妻感情甚笃，且一直支持丈夫对自由民主及人权理念的追求；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾为丈夫因涉嫌香港占中运动被中共当局抓捕而维权；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因丈夫发表《修宪公民建议书》，提出删除“宪法序言”等政治改革建议，而被北京市石景山警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被江苏省徐州市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年才刑满获释，遂其为寻求正义而为丈夫身陷囹圄不断呼吁和维权；然而因其为夫维权发声被中共当局视为需要监控和打压的维稳对象，故而频遭当局骚扰和虐待；后在众多维权律师、正义人士及维权公民的鼎力支持、帮助下，以及在德国驻华大使馆官员和欧盟驻中国代表团等的关注、呼吁下，最终度过其人生中最艰困的时刻，并与被囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年刑满出狱的丈夫得以团聚；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因余文生许艳夫妇二人受邀参加欧盟驻华代表团座谈会见，在前往会见的途中被北京市石景山八角派出所警方拦截传唤，后即失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇均被石景山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其二人又被以同罪名转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余文生代理律师到看守所要求与其会见遭到拒绝，随后被告知余文生涉罪又被新增“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初获悉，余文生及其妻子许艳被从北京转至苏州关押，目前余文生关押于苏州市第一看守所，许艳关押于同地点的苏州市第四看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，许艳寻衅滋事案开庭，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日宣判，许艳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/319.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/319.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162565472;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秦、陈品霖、任志强、董瑶琼、朱玉芳、涂金灿、许志永<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人狱中动态信息通报：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秦</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江苏人权捍卫者徐秦女士狱中情况通报——身体出现很多病症不能远走、快走<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，本网获悉：昨天律师会见了徐秦。徐秦说虽然现在看守所里对她的生活多有照顾，但长时间的拘押还是使得她身体出现很多病症。头部脑梗症状比以前更严重了，心率快，血压高。最近有点感冒咳嗽。看守所目前的生活和医疗条件都不适合她改善身体健康情况。目前，她不能远走、快走。她感谢朋友们和外界对她的关心和关注。徐秦经过<span lang="EN-US">12</span>次延期审理，一审被刑四年。二审如不改判，将于<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出狱。目前关押江苏省扬州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐秦简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，民间维权组织“中国人权观察”前秘书长，“玫瑰团队”成员，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。长期以来，一直关注中国人权状况，并与著名人权活动家、民主异议人士秦永敏一道筹建中国人权观察；自秦永敏被捕、秦之妻子赵素利“被失踪”后，她曾多次上街声援，跟进案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被警方突然限制自由，之后一直遭跟踪与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其在从扬州高邮到昆山的途中被警方带走，后得知其被扬州市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其家属委托的代理律师要求会见，遭到警方拒绝，但被告知其已于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日由刑拘转为“指定居所监视居住”；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又被追加罪名，以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续扣留，且不准律师会见；据悉，此次被捕，皆与其近年来坚持关注人权问题，后又积极组织联署声援维权律师余文生，以及为维权公民徐琳筹款等活动有关；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获悉，其已获取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，徐秦突然又被警方从家中带走；据悉，之前其案件一直处于延审中；此次被捕前，徐秦刚做完心脏搭桥手术，且患有脑梗、心梗、高血压等多种疾病。狱中身体状况急剧恶化，甚至瘫痪无法站立。后在律师的抗争和各界关注下，徐秦身体比以前好了一些，在别人的搀扶下可以走一小会。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份看守所安排她到东方医院做了检查，开了一些药。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日徐秦案已经在扬州市看守所法庭召开庭前会议，但长时间仍不开庭审理。徐秦案被延期审理竟然达到十二次，中共政权玩弄法律的肆无忌惮，令世人叹为观止。徐秦案终于在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午于扬州市中级人民法院开庭宣判，法庭判决徐秦犯煽动颠覆国家政权罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。目前徐秦被羁押于江苏省扬州市看守所。<b>信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/4_30.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/09/4_30.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">白纸运动之《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片制作人陈品霖（网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>）狱中境况通报： 在看守所中遭到不人道对待！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，本网获悉：被羁押的《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片制作人陈品霖（网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>）在看守所中遭到不人道对待。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖的代理律师袁茂在<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日发微博称：陈品霖在看守所中遭到不人道对待，包括极其拥挤的睡觉条件，以及一个月才放一次风。在他们前往住所检察官处反应情况时，检察官也不见踪影。陈品霖所遭受的不人道关押违反了《看守所条例》（第二十五条规定，人犯每日应当有必要的睡眠时间和一至两小时的室外活动）和《中华人民共和国看守所条例实施办法》（第二十七条规定，人犯居住的监室面积平均每人不得少于二平方米）。中共当局是《禁止酷刑和其他残忍、不人道或有辱人格的待遇或处罚公约》的缔约方，有义务保证陈品霖在被关押期间的待遇符合国内与国际标准，确保陈品霖和其律师的申诉得到公正的调查处理，并确保他们不会因申诉遭到任何虐待和恐吓。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><a name="_Hlk181065975"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈品霖</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名<span lang="EN-US">Plato</span>，白纸运动《乌鲁木齐中路》记录片制作人。生于<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，福建省霞浦县人。在习近平政府推行疯狂清零政策三年期间，中国人民的日常生活和自由遭受到严重的侵害。而新疆乌鲁木齐发生的一场大火彻底将民众对防疫政策的不满点燃。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，当上海人民自发的聚集街头悼念火灾中逝去的同胞时，没人料到这场悼念活动将引发全国范围內对防疫政策的抗议。陈品霖在上海现场拍摄大量视频、制作了《乌鲁木齐中路》纪录片，纪录片再现了民众自发参加悼念乌鲁木齐火灾遇难者，进而演变为要求解封并提出政治诉求的“白纸运动”的过程和场面。陈品霖在白纸运动一周年之际（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬）将纪录片上传到网络，不到一周，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，即遭抓捕，而其推特和<span lang="EN-US">Youtube</span>频道被销号。据悉与其一同被抓还有一位女生，后女生获取保，但陈品霖遭遭刑事拘留，后于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被上海市公安局宝山分局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被正式批捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。目前其案已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日由上海市宝山区检察院向上海市宝山区法院提起公诉。根据起诉书，陈品霖于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚在上海乌鲁木齐中路用手机拍摄并保存“<span lang="EN-US">11.26</span>”事件现场视频资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月开始制作《乌鲁木齐中路》白纸运动一周年完整回顾纪录片，于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日制作完成，通过多个境外平台推广，其中推特浏览量达<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万次。被指控“明知是编造的虚假信息，在信息网络上散布，造成公共秩序严重混乱；转发引用辱骂国家领导人言论，损害国家形象、严重危害国家利益”。陈品霖现被羁押在上海宝山区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/plato.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/plato.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任志强：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任志强女儿公开致信习近平 请求允许病重父亲出国治疗<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，本网获悉：任志强女儿公开致信习近平，请求允许病重父亲出国治疗。全文如下：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">“尊敬的习近平主席：您好！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">我是任志强的女儿，我恳请您基于人道主义原则，允许我父亲保外就医并出国治疗，让他在生命的最后时光中能够与家人团聚，得到应有的治疗和照顾。我的父亲在入狱前就已被诊断出患有严重的前列腺疾病，急需手术治疗。自入狱以来，他一直未能得到手术和有效的治疗，病情不断恶化。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">长期以来，他每天夜里需要去十几次洗手间，饱受病痛折磨，无法正常休息。最近几个月，他又被诊断出哮喘，健康状况每况愈下。我们多次恳求，但依然不被允许手术治疗，这让我们深感痛苦和绝望。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">我的哥哥也因父亲的案件被牵连，遭到重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。父亲入狱四年来，我们一家从未有过真正的团聚。疾病和判决让我们的家庭几近破碎，接近家破人亡。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">作为一个残破家庭的女儿，我希望能够为父亲争取到最后的人道治疗机会，恳请国家能够体现出对生命的起码尊重和最基本的人道关怀，允许我的父亲保外就医，出国治疗，在亲人的陪伴下安静度过余下的岁月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">我愿意承诺，我父亲出国治疗后绝不会公开发表任何言论或内容。他已年逾古稀，重病缠身，没有任何能力对您及国家带来麻烦。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">习近平主席，此前我们曾按照正常渠道数次提出上述诉求，始终没有得到善意回应，不得已只好用这种方式向您反映我们濒临绝望的诉求。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">请给我父亲一个出国治疗的机会，这不仅是对一个家庭最后希望的守护，也是对一个生命的尊重。一个宽容而富有同理心的决定，将会成为历史对您仁慈与胸襟的见证，而非留下令人痛心的遗憾。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">此致敬礼！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任志强的女儿<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>二零二四年十月二日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任志强简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">著名退休企业家、公众人物。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，绰号任大炮，男，籍贯山东莱州，中国企业家，历任北京市华远地产董事长、华远集团党委副书记兼董事长、北京市商业银行（北京银行前身）监事、新华保险董事。后退休。持有中国人民大学法律硕士学位。曾任北京市政协委员。父亲任泉生曾任商业部副部长。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，中共北京市纪律检查委员会、北京市监察委员会发布消息，称北京市华远集团原党委副书记、董事长任志强涉嫌严重违纪违法，目前正接受北京市西城区纪委区监委纪律审查和监察调查。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，北京市西城区纪委监察委发布通告，称任志强因严重违反共产党五项纪律，构成严重职务违法，涉嫌贪污、受贿、挪用公款、国有公司人员滥用职权犯罪，宣布开除任志强党籍处分，同时取消其的待遇，收缴违纪违法所得，涉嫌犯罪问题将移送检察机关依法审查起诉，所涉财物随案移送司法机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午九点三十分在北京市第二中级人民法院第九法庭开庭审理，任志强因言获罪被中共当局指控涉嫌贪污罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>受贿罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>挪用公款罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>国有企业人员滥用职权罪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪。庭审中任志强一言不发，表达抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，任志强被习近平当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，举世震惊。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_4.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董瑶琼：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被关精神病院已超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月的泼墨女<a name="_Hlk181068142">董瑶琼</a>目前仍音信全无、生死不明 其父董建彪狱中被迫害致死也已<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，本网获悉：被关精神病院已超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月的泼墨女董瑶琼目前仍音信全无、生死不明，其父董建彪狱中迫害致死也已<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多。六年多前——<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，勇敢的湖南女孩董瑶琼在上海市海航大厦前直播其对中共独裁专制的不满，并批评当局对百姓实施洗脑逼迫，大独裁者习近平的头像泼洒墨汁，这一事件被称为：董瑶琼泼墨习近平事件。董瑶琼随即在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被抓捕。此事件获全国声援，其被释放后不久董瑶琼三次被关进精神病医院，因父亲营救两次短暂被放出来。最后一次是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初，因董瑶琼的母亲配合当局，签字将自己健康的女儿送进精神病医院，当地“政府”给董母建了一栋房子。董瑶琼父亲董建彪愤怒斥责董瑶琼母亲丧尽天良，要求她接女儿出院，发生冲突，竟然惹来牢狱之灾和杀身之祸。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日董建彪惨死在狱中。而董建彪的亲属接通知后，赶到停尸房，发现董建彪尸体上有伤，而且国保要求尸体<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天内火化。距今董建彪狱中被迫害致死已经整整<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多了。目前，被关精神病院已超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月的泼墨女董瑶琼处于强迫失踪状态，生死不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董瑶琼简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1989</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市攸县桃水镇人，原上海房地产公司中介职员，推特名：<span lang="EN-US">feefeefly</span>，人称“泼墨女孩”，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因用<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>在上海市海航大厦前直播其对中共独裁专制的不满，并批评当局对百姓实施洗脑逼迫，并对中共最高领导人习近平的头像泼洒墨汁，进而引起社会广泛热议；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被上海市警方抓捕，自此失联，其推特账号被人关闭；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被上海市警方送回湖南省攸县老家，并以疑有“精神病”为由被变相关押于株洲市第三医院，直至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日其父在株洲市第三医院与女儿见面之后，方知其泼墨行为已被当局定性为“攻击国家领导人”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，取保释放，并被送到湖南省攸县桃水镇母亲住处；据悉，拘押期间曾备受酷刑虐待，关精神病院时被强迫吃药；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初，其再度被失踪，后被疑指已第三度关进株洲市第三精神病医院，至今未予释放；据悉，其推特内容已被人清空；其父董建彪为救女儿多次声明董瑶琼没有精神病，为其维权，最后被关进监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日董建彪惨死在狱中。董建彪的亲属接通知后，赶到停尸房，发现董建彪尸体上有伤，而且国保要求尸体<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天内火化。目前董瑶琼疑似被羁押于株洲市第三精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/38-2.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/38-2.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk181070083"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士<a name="_Hlk181069981">朱玉芳</a>狱中持续受病痛折磨，江西女子监狱坚持拒绝其外出就医<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。本网近日获悉：被以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士朱玉芳，目前在江西女子监狱持续受病痛折磨，其本就患有慢性疾病，又在今年年初遭到同监舍犯人殴打，头部、胸部、手部受到重创，由于没有得到有效治疗，留下严重后遗症，受创部位持续疼痛，手部关节至今无法弯曲，实际处于残疾状态。因为在狱中得不到有效治疗，朱玉芳多次要求狱方带其外出就医，但江西女子监狱以达不到外出就医条件为由，坚持拒绝带其外出就医。维权网呼吁江西女子监狱本着人道主义，允许朱玉芳外出就医，使其疾病得到有效治疗。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳是江西萍乡的强拆维权者。曾是经营<span lang="EN-US">4</span>家店面的私营业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年拆迁中，萍乡市政府主要领导亲属开办的房地产公司拒不兑现拆迁协议，朱玉芳被迫走上维权之路。在维权过程中，她不仅自己维权，也积极帮助他人维权，呼吁社会公正，遂被地方政府视为重点维稳控制和打击对象，被多次截访绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，朱玉芳因在北京身穿“没有腐败就没有访民”的文化衫维权，被北京警方抓走，转交给江西萍乡安源区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，朱玉芳一直为被枉法冤判而申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，她到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，遂在法院门外举牌呼吁；一周后的<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（世界人权日），朱玉芳就被萍乡市警方抓捕，随即被以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱玉芳第二次被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑，这次刑期比上次更长——<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。上诉后，萍乡市中级法院二审裁决维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。朱玉芳因为被枉法判刑而申诉喊冤，结果却遭到更大打击，被加重判刑。中共当局的司法由此可见一斑。江西省女子监狱地址：江西省南昌市新建县长堎镇长征路<span lang="EN-US">630</span>号江西省女子监狱，电话：<span lang="EN-US">0791-83718743</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/4_15.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/4_15.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">涂金灿：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京资深民间出版人<a name="_Hlk181070164">涂金灿</a>被控涉嫌“非法经营”案又被退回公安补充侦查<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。本网近日获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底被以“非法经营罪”刑事拘留的北京民间出版人涂金灿，其案卷又被退回北京市海淀区公安局进行所谓“补充侦查”。此前在今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底该案被公安移送北京海淀区检察院审查起诉，此后一度传出因涉及所谓“敏感”可能会被秘密开庭审理。而该案第一次在公安局侦查期间，已经被北京海淀区公安局两次延长侦查期限。从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月底涂金灿被以“非法经营罪”刑事拘留，案发至今已近一年，其间多次被延长侦查期限。此次该案又重新被退回公安进行所谓“侦查”，显示出中共当局控制下的司法，即使证据不足，也要罗织罪名，不把无罪者送进监狱不罢休的顽固意志。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">涂金灿简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1962</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生于湖北省孝感市，曾做过教师，后进行文化创业。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">,</span>涂金灿在北京创办“家谱传记机构”<span lang="EN-US">,</span>从事民间家谱、家史、传记的出书业务<span lang="EN-US">,</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被捕的<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年间<span lang="EN-US">,</span>已经为<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>多个普通百姓家庭整理出版了家谱、家史、个人传记类图书。他的事迹曾被新华社、《中国青年报》、《中国日报海外版》等官方媒体做过专题报道。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">,</span>时任总理李克强到海淀区创业大街视察<span lang="EN-US">,</span>还曾参观过涂金灿的“北京家谱传记文化馆”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年的三年疫情封控期间，涂金灿的民间出版业务遭到重大打击，仅靠借债勉强维持运作。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年疫情封控解除后，本以为业务能得到一些恢复，但当局的文化管制和经济勒索接踵而来。在被捕前，涂金灿已多次被海淀区文化部门、公安部门约谈，被海淀区公安局及中关村派出所查封图书仓库，公司承接的一部《何氏家谱》图书在邮寄发货后被海关查扣，以此为由进行罚款，但经过三年疫情，涂金灿及其公司已经债务累累，公司日常运作已经非常困难，根本没钱交纳罚款。当局的经济勒索没达到目的，就悍然动用司法手段，以刑事罪名抓捕了涂金灿，查封了“北京家谱传记机构”，导致公司停业员工失业。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_16.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许志永：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年著名人权捍卫者许志永狱中绝食已<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天 体重短时间内下降<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多斤<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，本网获悉：为了抗议鲁南监狱及相关人员的违法行为、捍卫通信权。著名人权捍卫者许志永从<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日至今，已经绝食整<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天了，体重在短时间内下降了<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多斤。今年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，就曾传出许志永在鲁南监狱狱中被酷刑：名字被消失、被强迫劳动、精神虐待、被剥夺通信权以及被变相单独关押。维权网强烈要求中共当局立即停止对许志永的酷刑，保障其基本人权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">许志永简介：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1973</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，河南省商丘市民权县人，前北京邮电学院专业讲师，前北京市海淀区人民法院人民陪审员，“公盟”重要创始人，青年法学家、宪政学者和公民维权代理人，就全国人大对《城市流浪乞讨人员收容遣送办法》进行违宪审查提议者，新公民运动倡导者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其被北京市警方以涉嫌“聚扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘，关押在北京市第三看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，许志永被广州市警方从番禺海鸥岛杨斌律师处带走；据悉，其此次被抓，此与<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月曾因参加“厦门聚会案”遭通缉有关，许志永自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日丁家喜律师被捕后就一直在中国南方秘密流亡。其亲友均遭多次骚扰跟踪，其女友李翘楚亦被强迫失踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，许志永被以涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪正式逮捕，曾羁押于山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，许志永遭中共当局以颠覆国家政权罪判处<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年重刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。其不服上诉，二审遭驳回，维持原判。许志永二审后已转监到位于山东日照的鲁南监狱服刑。鲁南监狱地址：山东省日照市东港区南湖镇西黄山前村西<span lang="EN-US">500</span>米。其邮寄地址：山东省日照市<span lang="EN-US">979</span>信箱<span lang="EN-US">15</span>分箱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/1420-10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-spacerun: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">本期新增被刑事拘留及被精神病的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span></span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></a></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭宏英、李学惠、易惠军、许冬青、杨丽、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">涂强：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川自贡市异议人士，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">36</span>岁。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因为辱骂毛泽东及<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初在网上发布了纪念“八九六四学运”以及呼吁中国实现自由民主的贴文被家人配合警察强行送入过自贡第五人民医院精神科。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日涂强在微朋友圈发信息说：“这次我又被警察政治迫害。关押四川自贡市精神病医院已经七个月了，他们还不说什么时候放我出来，肯定定打算长期关押我。”此外涂强给网友发私信表示自己还在“五医院”，派出所不给他出去，因为他母亲去看他才得以用手机发信息。根据此前民生观察自愿者对涂强的采访记录，涂强所说的“五医院”应该是“自贡市第五人民医院精神病科”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">网名赵未。男，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住山东省聊城市东昌府区。其曾因言获罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>被控煽动颠覆国家政权罪抓捕，被手铐脚镣铁椅，监视居住六个月。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日送聊城看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日开庭，后又被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，指控其<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年来网络言论危害国家安全，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日刑满出狱。赵长慧<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月去北京被其街道主任拦截，发生冲突，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭刑事拘留、后于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被批捕，羁押于聊城看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪起诉，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日庭审<b>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/20241016.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、许宗平：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">青年人权律师张文鹏所涉海韵集团案同案。职务为海韵集团副总经理。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被决定逮捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日傍晚家属收到逮捕通知书。许宗平妻子小云待业，家里两个小孩，一个读幼儿园，一个读小学一年级。许宗平目前羁押于海南省三亚市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk181069309">卢思位</a>：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">973</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，四川省知名人权律师，办理过成都纪念「八九六四」酒案，是成都「四君子」之一张隽勇的辩护人，曾代理十二港人“偷渡案”、余文生 、王藏 、覃永沛 、陈家鸿 等“煽动颠覆国家政权案”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，卢思位律师就发起公民联署，呼吁全国人大成立特别调查委员会，就“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”系列案件是否存在强迫服药等酷刑进行独立调查，调查委员会的组成人员应当包括律师和公民代表，并向公开调查结论。厦门聚会案发生后，卢思位律师受到传唤及威胁，并被禁止出境。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日卢思位律师因办理过广西律师陈家鸿「煽动颠覆国家政权案」，曾遭受四川司法当局和律师协会打压和处分。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，余文生律师因煽动颠覆国家政权罪成，被徐州市中级法院判处徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，卢思位律师作为二审辩护人参与辩护工作。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，有十二位香港社运人士被深圳公安扣押在盐田看守所，卢思位律师曾经探访十二位被扣押香港人，又向他们提供法律援助。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日成都市羊青区司法局对卢思位律师代理的所有案件材料检查。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，四川省司法厅对卢思位律师开出行政处罚案件当事人听证权利告知书，准备吊销卢律师的律师执业证。后卢思位遭吊销律师证。卢思位先生于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午在准备登上一列开往泰国的火车时，被老挝警方逮捕。卢思位的原定行程是在泰国搭乘班机前往美国与家人团聚。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月卢思位被老挝政府连同其他<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名中国人，一起分乘两辆车，遣返中国。随后，卢思位被中共当局关押到四川成都市新都看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，卢思位律师取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，卢思位被传唤到保和派出所做了三个小时左右的笔录，随后被告知，他的案子将由成华区公安局移送成华区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其再遭抓捕。目前羁押于成都看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_11.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_11.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk181069592">刘家玲</a>：天</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">津市静海区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁。原是静海区市容环卫局的干部。早年修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，她因坚持修炼法轮大法，被开除公职，并几次身陷囹圄，曾两次被劳教共计<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年：刘家玲女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年两次被劳教，关押到天津大港区板桥女子劳教所，共<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，期间遭强制奴役劳动、不让睡觉等迫害。她丈夫在中共的强大压力下与她离婚。两次被判刑共计<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年半：<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年刘家玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，在天津女子监狱，她遭到体罚、洗脑、奴役等酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月下旬，刘家玲又遭抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半，再次被劫持到天津女子监狱迫害。她约于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月下旬结束冤刑。出狱后，刘家玲就向有关部门申请要回被非法扣除的工资和退休金，这本是一个公民拥有的正当权利，却于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月又一次遭到中共当局的抓捕。她被关押在静海区看守所，至今已有一年多。据悉，刘家玲在看守所为维护自己的合法权利，绝食抗议，瘦弱不堪，现已生命垂危。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_57.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
