lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk181069778">郭宏英</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，吉林省四平市人，四平市铁东区海银花园小区居民，下岗工人，维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因其兄郭洪伟举报吉林省龙潭区检察院控申科长和其亲友虚开公款票据，遭打击报复被捕入狱冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其兄不服，出狱后随多次携母一同进京上访投诉，再遭地方当局打压，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月母子二人均被刑拘、逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其兄（郭洪伟）和其母亲（肖蕰苓）分别被吉林省四平市铁东区法院枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，且服刑其间，母子二人因多次出现病危，请求保外就医遭拒；为了给亲人讨回公道，其勇敢维权，并因长期驻京投诉和积极参与各种维权活动，遂又遭地方当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，曾因到长春市向吉林省“两会”代表递送伸冤材料，而被维稳人员拦截绑架；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，又因去探监看望其兄，而被四平市警方以“越级上访，殴打他人”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑拘；一个月后，被四平市检察院起诉，且新增“寻衅滋事罪”；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其案在吉林省四平市铁东区法院开庭受理，两天后被以“妨碍公务罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月）、“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年），二罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经吉林省四平市中院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。曾在吉林省长春女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日郭宏英去北京联系二次尸检被四平市公安局铁东分局强行押回，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日即被铁东分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，羁押于四平市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_15.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_15.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk181078271">李学惠</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京人权捍卫者、强拆受害者。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年他家房子遭政府强拆没给任何补偿，他被迫依法上访维权却屡遭政府的打击迫害，被行政拘留、刑事拘留、强迫旅游达数十次之多。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年他在看守所内被迫在政府主导的赔偿协议上签字，并被警方押解带着枷锁去看房。出狱后李学惠为了捍卫自己做人的尊严，对这种解决方式提出抗议继续上访维权，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年他被构陷罪名劳动教养一年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李学惠帮助北京奥运劳教老人八十多岁的王秀英录制发布了以行为艺术的形式进行上访的视频。视频发出后两天，即<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，王秀英及其女儿王凤仙被当局带走失踪，紧接着视频发布者李学惠也被带走失踪。后李学惠被北京警方指控在北京“奥运劳教老人”王秀英拍摄的行为艺术视频事件中起到组织策划、协助拍摄、消息发布等作用，因而涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被警方拘捕，羁押石景山区看守所。后李学惠被以寻衅滋事案判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日获悉：<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月初，李学惠因创作发布<span lang="EN-US">AI</span>维权视频遭刑事拘留，具体详情待查。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_66.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_66.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<a name="_Hlk181078718">易惠军</a>：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南株洲民主人士，中国公民党代理总裁<span lang="EN-US">,1966</span>年生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>湖南株洲人。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，<a name="_Hlk181078591">湖南株洲民主人士易惠军</a>发布了《中国公民党宣言》，<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日当地警方闻讯到他家来找他，今天其多位朋友给其打电话，已无人接听，大概率已被抓捕。 易惠军在其撰写的《中国公民党宣言》中写到：“<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日是中国公民党宣布成立之日！易惠军任首任中国公民党代理总裁。”“中国公民党的目标是：达成中国免费教育、免费医疗、免费养老，取消退休双轨制，人人平等。实行一人一票，两院制、三权分立。多党竞选上岗执政。将所有机构的党委彻底剥离，减轻纳税人负担。”该宣言最后写道：“天下苦秦久矣！这句活用在<span lang="EN-US">CCP</span>（中共）统治下的中国实在恰如其分。一党执政七十多年实在乏善可陈，就连体制内的前总理温家宝都强烈呼吁政治体制改革。 本党就是在这种环境下应运而生。公民党是一位共产党员提议，他解释道是每个人都能够被公平的对待。可见共产党内也有许多人怨声载道。宣言还强调说：本党旨在参政论政造福人民，请现任执政党不要将颠覆国家政权罪扣在本党头上。国家依旧在，只是独裁亡！<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span>中国公民党总裁：易惠军<span lang="EN-US">2024.10.14 </span>左手书。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_62.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_62.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、许冬青：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏访民，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，流亡日本的维权人士杨彩英今日通报：“现在，我<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁心脏病重症母亲许冬青和肾病<span lang="EN-US">4</span>期妹妹杨丽因上访控告江苏当局违法征地、省市官员田洪和陈金虎侵犯人权不让看病、金坛区委书记陆秋明和副区长姚祥非法扣押被诈骗资金<span lang="EN-US">130</span>万拒不归还，双双被金坛当局涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。”</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;"> </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省常州市金坛区重病访民许冬青（<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁、患重症心脏病、高血压）和女儿杨丽（<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁、肾衰竭）因上访控告江苏当局违法征地、公安违法办案，遭江苏省社会工作部部长田洪、常州市市委书记陈金虎下令截访拦访不准看病。随后，许冬青、杨丽母女无数次遭到金坛公安的绑架殴打和刑事、行政拘留。从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月上访至今，杨丽被被刑讯逼供、被殴打至昏迷、被公安威胁要开车撞死用刀捅死、被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次。其父杨国良被公安砸伤住院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许冬青因向习近平求助被金坛公安刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天，期间有病不给治、被禁止上厕所、被脱光羞辱、被投喂大量不明药物。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，许冬青因上访再次被金坛公安刑拘。当日晚上，送达刑事拘留通知书的金坛滨湖派出所副所长翟俊侃称先拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日后如何处理由领导开会决定。至今、许冬青依然被拘押在常州看守所中。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，杨丽到北京反映冤情后被送到久敬庄接济服务中心。次日，金坛驻京办倪卫兵带黑社会冲入该中心将杨丽绑回金坛，在被金坛滨湖派出所拘押<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时后在<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日中午放回。当日晚上，滨湖派出所副所长翟俊侃打电话要求杨丽去派出所，杨丽没有理睬他。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，金坛区西城街道办事处主任栾留康和常州市公安局国保漆明智派出的送饭人员将杨丽骗出，后杨丽一直处于失联状态。傍晚，金坛滨湖派出所民警电话通知其父杨国良，称杨丽涉嫌寻衅滋事被拘押。许冬青、杨丽母女在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年上访后，江苏官员除了田洪、陈金虎下令截访拦访不让看病，金坛区委书记陆秋明、副区长姚祥、江苏省信访局办公室主任王春明等对待信访问题一直躺平不作为。其中、陆秋明和姚祥更是非法扣押杨国良被诈骗资金<span lang="EN-US">130</span>万元拒不归还。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_21.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、杨丽：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏访民，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，流亡日本的维权人士杨彩英今日通报：“现在，我<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁心脏病重症母亲许冬青和肾病<span lang="EN-US">4</span>期妹妹杨丽因上访控告江苏当局违法征地、省市官员田洪和陈金虎侵犯人权不让看病、金坛区委书记陆秋明和副区长姚祥非法扣押被诈骗资金<span lang="EN-US">130</span>万拒不归还，双双被金坛当局涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。”</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体;"> </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省常州市金坛区重病访民许冬青（<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁、患重症心脏病、高血压）和女儿杨丽（<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁、肾衰竭）因上访控告江苏当局违法征地、公安违法办案，遭江苏省社会工作部部长田洪、常州市市委书记陈金虎下令截访拦访不准看病。随后，许冬青、杨丽母女无数次遭到金坛公安的绑架殴打和刑事、行政拘留。从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月上访至今，杨丽被被刑讯逼供、被殴打至昏迷、被公安威胁要开车撞死用刀捅死、被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次。其父杨国良被公安砸伤住院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，许冬青因向习近平求助被金坛公安刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天，期间有病不给治、被禁止上厕所、被脱光羞辱、被投喂大量不明药物。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，许冬青因上访再次被金坛公安刑拘。当日晚上，送达刑事拘留通知书的金坛滨湖派出所副所长翟俊侃称先拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日后如何处理由领导开会决定。至今、许冬青依然被拘押在常州看守所中。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，杨丽到北京反映冤情后被送到久敬庄接济服务中心。次日，金坛驻京办倪卫兵带黑社会冲入该中心将杨丽绑回金坛，在被金坛滨湖派出所拘押<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时后在<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日中午放回。当日晚上，滨湖派出所副所长翟俊侃打电话要求杨丽去派出所，杨丽没有理睬他。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，金坛区西城街道办事处主任栾留康和常州市公安局国保漆明智派出的送饭人员将杨丽骗出，后杨丽一直处于失联状态。傍晚，金坛滨湖派出所民警电话通知其父杨国良，称杨丽涉嫌寻衅滋事被拘押。许冬青、杨丽母女在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年上访后，江苏官员除了田洪、陈金虎下令截访拦访不让看病，金坛区委书记陆秋明、副区长姚祥、江苏省信访局办公室主任王春明等对待信访问题一直躺平不作为。其中、陆秋明和姚祥更是非法扣押杨国良被诈骗资金<span lang="EN-US">130</span>万元拒不归还。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_21.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/blog-post_21.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省鹤岗市萝北县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，家住黑龙江省鹤岗市萝北县延军农垦社区<span lang="EN-US">C</span>区。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，他在浙江省舟山市打工期间，仅因向一些小区粘贴印有二维码网址的不干胶，对群众宣讲法轮功，使用真相币，被抓捕、抄家。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。现在被关押在浙江省第四监狱。家人要去看望他，狱方说得马国斌本人发起邀请或者是到马国斌户籍所在地派出所开一个亲属证明才能接见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><a name="_Hlk181080191"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181080191;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、伊克拉木</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181080191;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;微软雅黑&quot;,sans-serif; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑;">・</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181080191;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体;">努尔买买提（维）：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181080191;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1991</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生，新疆乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Ikram Nurmehmet</span>，北京常居公民，独立电影导演兼制作人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年曾出国留学，到土耳其的马尔马拉大学攻读电视电影艺术系相关专业；期间，其母亲还曾在<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年专程前往土耳其探望他，但不料其母回国几年后竟遭中共当局翻旧帐，疑其出国与政治活动有染，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被抓捕和判处<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年监禁，且于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年刑满后仍被关进“再教育营”（国际上常称“集中营”）不放；其父亲亦曾被关进集中营，至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年获释时已被折磨出一身伤害，三个月后因病去世；其于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年大学毕业后返回国内，因专业喜好而力主关注少数民族题材，并在北京常居，作导演、制作短纪录片和纪录式节目等工作，其制作短片《拼车》等作品，至今仍可在<span lang="EN-US">FIRST</span>影展组委会网站看到；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其突遭中共警方的“会面要求”（实为传唤），令其澄清一些有关“案件的事实”，之后即被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方强行带至机场返回新疆；据悉，前往机场的途中，警方曾电话其妻，称他是“恐怖份子”，需返疆受审，让她尽快带上丈夫的衣物送到机场；后其妻在机场见到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名公安中的一人，将其婚戒和一个“护身符”交给其妻；而其母亦在其抵达新疆乌鲁木齐机场时，被警方告知其子正在“接受调查”，并送乌鲁木齐第一看守所关押；后其家人知其很快被逮捕、起诉，被控曾于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2016</span>年在土耳其留学期间“积极参加恐怖活动”；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其被新疆乌鲁木齐中级法院以疑似“领导、参加恐怖组织罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。据悉，其要私聘律师遭绝，官方指定律师在参加法院庭审时，才知其在法庭上表示，羁押期间其曾被关暗室长达<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天，惨遭刑讯逼供，而后官方就凭这些酷刑逼供出来的假口供和他持有的一张土耳其居住证即成重要罪证；并且尽管其父母及妻子当时均到庭旁听，但最终知道其被判刑期已过半年有余。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">安徽省阜阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年七十一岁，原阜阳市颍州区文峰社区医院妇产科医生。早年修炼法轮功。自一九九九年七月，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，范文芳遭到残酷迫害，多次被抓捕到看守所，两次被关押到洗脑班迫害，三次被劳教，三次被判刑（七年、五年、五年），期间遭到酷刑惨烈折磨，九死一生。范文芳被中共劳教、判刑累计时间长达二十年之久。范文芳<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在路上被警察抓捕，关押在阜阳市女子看守所，随后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。最后她再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。范文芳现今被关押在安徽省女子监狱十一监区。在安徽省女子监狱集训队时，范文芳不认罪、不转化、不唱红歌、不背监规，被集训队的事务犯群殴暴打。目前其在狱中被迫害致不能直立行走，满嘴无牙齿，靠喝流食维持生命。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北省秦皇岛市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，赵红梅与另一法轮功学员，去秦皇岛市开发区发放法轮功资料、张贴真相标语，遭人举报。警察通过监控摄像头录像对她追踪、监控。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日上午，赵红梅在老父亲家（秦皇岛市国兴蓝海湾小区）被开发区公安分局国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。赵红梅随即被关押在秦皇岛市看守所。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，赵红梅被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，随后被转监至河北省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省牡丹江市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年已六十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共发动对法轮功的迫害后，他曾在<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑入狱七年，狱中遭酷刑，身体被迫害致残。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，赵军在牡丹江文化广场养鸽处，给一年轻男子宣讲法轮功，被两个警察抓捕到牡丹江市东安分局新安派出所。随后，警察闯到赵军家抄家。后对赵军拘留十五天，因疫情期间，看守所不收。一年零十个月后，即<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，警方又因此事刑事拘留赵军。赵军被强制体检后，因血压过高，看守所又拒收。赵军在家被“监视居住”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，他被爱民区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款一万元。他上诉后，又被中级法院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，赵军被收监到公安医院所谓“治疗”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月上旬得知，赵军已被转监到齐齐哈尔市泰来监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">51</span>岁。其家住玉山县火车站附近，她原来在玉山县金山工业园区工作，在三清山绿色食品有限公司任出纳。她于一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>您朱兰慧曾被劳教一年半，在江西省南昌女子劳教所中遭受酷刑折磨。朱兰慧<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被<span lang="EN-US">610</span>国保入室抓捕，关押在上饶市看守所，狱中其绝食抗争。后获刑她已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被转监到监狱继续服刑。刑期至：<span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><a name="_Hlk181079804"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181079804;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陕西省西安市鄠邑区（原户县）法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁。家住西安市鄠邑区余下镇热电厂社区，原惠安集团惠安化工厂惠邦公司工程师。刘春霞因坚持修炼法轮功，先后两次被中共当局判刑，累计陷冤狱长达<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，刘春霞在西安市鄠邑区紫金大厦上班时，被西安市公安局鄠邑区分局国保大队、惠民路派出所以及西安市公安局国保警察抓捕，并将她挟持回家，抄走电脑、手机、大法书籍、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、真相币等私人财物。刘春霞被审讯后，被刑事拘留，押往西安市莲湖区看守所。她因体检血压高达<span lang="EN-US">234mmHg</span>，看守所拒收。之后她被关押到西安市安康医院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘春霞被西安市鄠邑区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘春霞从西安市安康医院被转监到莲湖区看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刘春霞被起诉至西安市莲湖区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刘春霞被西安市莲湖区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘春霞被转监至陕西省女子监狱服刑，家属已收到入监通知书。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk181067359;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New bold;">甘肃平凉市静宁县法轮功学员，男，静宁县八里镇闫庙学校的一名普通教师，于一九九四年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月二十日中共集团疯狂迫害法轮功后，二十多年来，王世军因为坚持修炼法轮功而被多次抓捕，曾遭劳教迫害三年，被判刑三年多，拘留过数次。狱中惨遭酷刑迫害。王世军<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭静宁县公安局国保大队警察抓捕，随即被刑事拘留，后遭批捕、起诉。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，他目前在兰州监狱服刑，据悉他被剥夺亲人探视的权利。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被三星口派出所警察抓捕、在青龙县看守所关押十天。郝丽萍<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日因发放法轮功资料被警察抓捕，刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东泰安市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁。原铁道部十四局集团驻山东省泰市第二有限公司职工医院的医生。她坚持修炼法轮功，被剥夺工作权利，多年来，她靠租房和经营服装维持生计。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午，付雁丽回家时被岱岳区公安分局政保大队抓捕，后被刑事拘留、批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，岱岳区检察院将她非法起诉到岱岳区法院。付雁丽于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被泰安市岱岳区法院庭审，庭审时关押折磨近十个月的付雁丽被法警架着进入审判庭。她骨瘦如柴、身体虚弱，已不能自己行走。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。付雁丽随即上诉至泰安市中级法院，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，泰安市中院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日下夜班回家，在自家小区内被五名警察拦截，他们扣留王宏车内未装订的《天赐洪福》等月刊半成品，并在当天将王宏关押到哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，律师到国保支队依法提出撤销王宏涉嫌利用“邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”一案并立即释放的要求；家属提出对王宏取保申请均被铁路公安处国保支队拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">辽宁沈阳法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，系沈阳五联商场电梯维修人员。他<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始修炼法轮功。刘国华<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被沈阳市公安局大东分局国保大队、大东门派出所警察抓捕、抄家。并遭刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘国华被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日他被起诉至沈阳市大东区法院。目前关押在沈阳市大东区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月得知，刘国华已被大东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/10/16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、毛德君：</span></b></span></span><span mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省临沂市莒南县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁。东北某中学的退休物理教师。她于一九九八年十月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月曾遭抓捕判刑，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日毛德君遭当地警方抓捕，非法审讯后被“取保候审”手续后，放她回家。后遭起诉、开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，临沭县法院通知毛德君去拿判决书。当天，毛德君在家属的陪伴下到临沭县法院，毛德君被判刑一年。随即毛德君被收监，现被关押在临沂看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark:
